// TOKENS
actor StatToken : Inventory 10050
{
	-INVBAR
	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	
	Scale 0.5
	
	Inventory.amount 1
	Inventory.MaxAmount 10000
	Inventory.PickupMessage "You got a Stat Token!"
	Inventory.PickupSound "items/vial"
	
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TOKA A 0 Bright A_PlaySound("hums/stat", CHAN_ITEM, 1.0, true, 4)
		TOKA ABCDEFGH 2 Bright
		Loop
	}
}

	}
